# About this item

- RAW GRASS FED WHEY PROTEIN: 100% Pure Grass Fed whey protein powder from the milk of jersey cows that graze freely on lush, green pastures year round. These small-farm cows are not only healthier but we believe happier too!
- 3RD PARTY LAB TESTED: We're proud to be able to say that our whey protein powder is tested at 3rd party laboratories to ensure there are no contaminants. We test for heavy metals, antibiotics, pesticides, mycotoxins & melamine. Additionally, all of our packaging is BPA free.
- ONLY 1 INGREDIENT: Unflavored Whey Protein Powder, No added sweeteners, preservatives or fillers. NO SOY lecithin & no sunflower lecithin. Processed WITHOUT acid or bleach.
- HIGHEST QUALITY: Our whey protein powder is Cold Processed, NON-GMO, Soy Free, rBGH/rBST Hormone Free, Gluten Free, Grass Fed and Heavy Metal Free.
- LESS PROCESSED: Whey protein concentrate is the least processed form of whey, which means it’s loaded with high-quality complete protein and essential amino acids.
- GRASS FED WHEY: Sourced 100% from US Sustainable Small Farms. Cow's diet consists of a variety of wild grasses and clover - producing milk rich in omega-3s and CLAs

## Product Description

Our jersey cows graze freely on lush, green pastures year round. These small farm cows are not only healthier but we believe happier too! Their diet consists of a variety of wild grasses and clover, producing milk rich in omega 3s and CLAs. The result is a deliciously creamy whey protein powder that has the highest protein concentration among natural grass fed whey powders. Raw Grass Fed Whey protein powder is minimally processed at low temperatures and is higher in antioxidants and other nutrients than conventional whey powders. Superior quality begins with what the cows eat and how they live, which is why our whey is sourced from jersey cows that are grass fed on small family farms in the US. We ensure that these cows are raised without hormones, antibiotics, steroids, or genetically modified feed, and they are Non GMO. Raw Grass Fed Whey tastes so amazing by itself, we don't add any sweeteners, flavors or fillers. Just 100% grass fed whey protein!

### Product Safety and Compliance DetailsProduct Safety and Compliance Details

### Safe use

As the [Food and Drug Administration (FDA)](https://www.fda.gov/media/158337/download?attachment) advises, dietary supplements can support your overall health but may also have powerful effects on the body. It’s important to read labels carefully, exercise caution, and consult your healthcare professional before taking any supplement. Side effects are more likely if supplements are taken in high doses, as substitutes for prescribed medications, or in combination with multiple supplements. If you experience severe side effects, discontinue use immediately and seek medical attention.

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say

Customers praise this protein powder's quality, noting it contains 84% protein and is made from a single ingredient with no additives or fillers. The powder mixes well in smoothies and has a creamy, smooth texture without chalkiness. They appreciate its health benefits, with one customer noting it's processed in the healthiest way possible. While some customers find it good value for money, others consider it expensive.

- [![](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)\\

L. C.](https://www.amazon.com/gp/profile/amzn1.account.AGDBZFZHSDRAPI4A35HGCIE2K4OA/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_gw_tr?ie=UTF8)





##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ Clean, grassfed whey protein for athletes-- at a fair price](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R8QI297A0IWGH/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)



Reviewed in the United States on May 15, 2025

Size: 5 Pound (Pack of 1) [Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)






We use a LOT of protein powder-- ~ 5lbs a month, and this has become one of our go-to products (National Team athletes). The price is fair, especially for a grass-fed product, and it is high-quality and clean-- no additives, flavors, sweeteners, or emulsifiers in the Plain version. I use this daily in protein shakes of all sorts (pre-workout, meal replacement, recovery, pre-sleep) and having something without fake flavoring or sweeteners gives me all sorts of flexibility to make things work for my tastes and purposes. We also use this to bake with, as it is very neutral in flavor and works well in healthier bars, brownies, etc. It smells clean and fresh, like a milk protein should, and does not have added sugar. Calories are in line with other non-flavored whey powders. Be aware that because this whey has no added ingredients and does not use emulsifiers or lecithins, it does require a blender bottle or mixer to blend fast. If you don't use a blender bottle or mixer, you can put it in the water/ liquid, give it a stir and let it sit for 5-10 minutes, and it will be easier to mix in.

But that's a very small issue, especially considering how well this protein powder works and how clean it is. If you like the fancier flavors like Belgian Chocolate or Birthday Cake, then this is not the product for you (unless of course you are blending your own flavors :-D). But if you want something clean, pure, high quality, and fairly priced-- this is the one.

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ Just Whey](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/RYPS4QTRFZ33T/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)



Reviewed in the United States on February 22, 2025

Size: 12 Ounce (Pack of 1) [Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)






Wow! I'm so impressed with this whey! I've tried a lot of different brands of whey protein powders over the past 25 years. Anywhere from brands you can get at the big box stores, to specialty brands you could only get at health food stores and even a few subscription based ones only gym bros knew about. Seriously, if you name it, I've probably tried it.



I haven't used whey protein shakes as part of my diet for the past couple years. I just kind of got away from them. But after a visit with a functional health professional, I was in the market looking for a whey protein powder to supplement my diet as I need more protein in my diet but can't eat anymore meat than I already do.



I appreciate that this whey is JUST whey. No lecithin. No synthetic sugar substitutes. No "natural flavors". No hidden additives, just whey.



This whey protein was easy to use in my shake, digested well with zero effects. No stomach upset. It has NO taste. I appreciate I was able to buy a smaller bag in case I didn't like it.



For me, I haven't noticed excessive foaming like some reviewers mentioned. I mixed mine in whole raw milk though. I'm not sure if maybe the others experiencing lots of foam were using water or a nut milk?



The other thing I noticed is, it doesn't mix well by hand in cold or hot . Not a deal breaker for me as I usually always use my blender. But I did try to add it to my hot coffee like a powdered creamer and it didn't work.



My favorite recipe I've been making with this whey is:

10 oz whole (raw) milk

25g grass fed whey

1 TBS Cacao powder

1/2 TBS King Arthur malted milk (cleanest brand I can find)

Combine with blender, poor over ice, enjoy



Thank you to Raw Grass Fed Whey for making a pure whey product for a reasonable price!

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ Great tasting protein !](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R102H7DR6C8FIN/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)



Reviewed in the United States on January 21, 2025

Size: 5 Pound (Pack of 1) [Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)






I’ve been using the Raw Grass Fed Gluten-Free Whey Protein Powder for a few years now, and overall, I’m very impressed. Here’s a breakdown of the pros and cons:



Pros:



High-Quality Ingredients: This protein powder is made from grass-fed whey, so I feel good knowing it’s sourced from cows raised on a natural diet without hormones or antibiotics.



Gluten-Free: Perfect for those with gluten sensitivities or those following a gluten-free diet. No issues with digestion here.



Clean Label: Minimal ingredients, which is great if you're avoiding unnecessary additives, sweeteners, or fillers. It’s also non-GMO, which is a huge plus for me.



Good Taste: The flavor is mild and not overly sweet, which I appreciate. It mixes well with water, almond milk, or smoothies.



High Protein Content: With a solid amount of protein per serving, this powder helps with muscle recovery and can be a great post-workout supplement.



Easily Digestible: No bloating or discomfort after consumption. I’ve found it easy on my stomach, unlike some other protein powders.



Cons:



Price: It’s a bit on the higher side compared to other whey protein powders, but I’m willing to pay for the quality.



Taste Can Be Bland for Some: While I like the taste, others may find it too subtle or bland if they prefer more flavor or sweetness.



Overall, I highly recommend the Raw Grass Fed Gluten-Free Whey Protein Powder for anyone looking for a clean, high-quality protein source. If you’re willing to invest in a slightly pricier product, you won’t be disappointed
